Projects API

[error] Create an invalid project

POST api/v1/projects

Parameters

Name Description
project[title_multiloc] The title of the project, as a multiloc string
project[description_multiloc] The description of the project, as a multiloc HTML string
project[slug] The unique slug of the project. If not given, it will be auto generated
project[header_bg] Base64 encoded header image
project[area_ids] Array of ids of the associated areas
project[topic_ids] Array of ids of the associated topics

Response Fields

Name Description
errors[title_multiloc] Array containing objects with signature {error: 'blank' | 'unsupported_locales' }
errors[description_multiloc] Array containing objects with signature {error: 'blank' | 'unsupported_locales' }
errors[slug] Array containing objects with signature {error: 'invalid' }
